    <div class="content-sidebar-wrap">
     <main class="content" itemprop="mainContentOfPage" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Blog" role="main">
      <article class="post-1411 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-appetizers category-dinner category-gluten-free category-meat entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         Champagne Turkey Meatballs
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2013-12-30T05:00:32+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
          December 30, 2013
         </time>
         by
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/author/davida" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Davida Kugelmass
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs.html#comments">
           105 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <p>
         Sorry, no weekend recap today! I know youre all devastated. I actually had a fantastic weekend, but I just didnt feel like capturing it. Ive noticed that I sometimes have a hard time living in the moment when I have my camera or phone. I get this messed up feeling that if it isnt photographed, it didnt actually happen. Clearly I have a problem.
         <a href="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs2.jpg">
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="champagne turkey meatballs" class="size-full wp-image-1417 aligncenter" height="1020" src="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs2.jpg" width="680"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://www.thehealthymaven.com/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs.html&amp;media=http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs2.jpg&amp;description=Champagne Turkey Meatballs')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </a>
         Im not entirely sure when things changed, but Ive somehow managed to develop an interest in photography. Remember when I did a whole post about
         <a href="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/2013/08/maple-oatmeal-cookies.html">
          food photography being the bane of my existence
         </a>
         ? Well, I take it back. Somewhere between then and now my camera and I became friends. It likely had something to do with the fact that I actually read the manualone year later.I want to clarify that I do NOT enjoy food photography when I am hangry. The pictures never turn out well because I am too impatient to keep trying to get the best shot. I can always tell when Ive taken a photo in a rush, but my stomach takes precedence no matter what.
         <a href="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs-21.jpg">
          <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
           <img alt="champagne turkey meatballs 2" class="size-full wp-image-1418 aligncenter" height="1020" src="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs-21.jpg" width="680"/>
           <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://www.thehealthymaven.com/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs.html&amp;media=http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs-21.jpg&amp;description=Champagne Turkey Meatballs')">
           </span>
          </span>
         </a>
         I have approximately 48 hours to overwhelm you with New Years recipes. I apologize in advance if I harass your twitter/facebook feeds reposting mine and my friends deliciousness. New Years is like the underdog to Christmas. Christmas gets a solid 6 weeks of build-up and New Years only a measly week. So Im giving it the credit it deserves. Today were doing a champagne turkey meatball appetizer, tomorrow a dessert and Wednesday youll be privy to my resolutions that Im attempting to not fail at this year. Stay tuned!
        </p>
        <div class="hrecipe f1">
         <p class="fn single_recipe_header" style="font-size: 18px; color: #b31212; padding: 0; margin: 5px 5px 5px 0px;">
          <strong>
           Champagne Turkey Meatballs
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          <img alt="" class="photo" src="http://www.recipage.com/images/user2282/1388359992/recipe_image.jpg" style="clear: both; float: left; width: 40%; padding: 0 10px 10px 0;"/>
         </p>
         <p class="single_recipe_text" id="author" style="font-size: 15px; color: #141517; padding: 0; margin: 5px 5px 5px 0px;">
          by
          <span class="author">
           The Healthy Maven
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="single_recipe_text" style="color: #141517; font-size: 12px; padding: 0; margin: 8px 4px 4px 4px;">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           Prep Time:
          </span>
          <span class="preptime">
           10 mins
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="single_recipe_text" style="color: #141517; font-size: 12px; padding: 0; margin: 4px;">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           Cook Time:
          </span>
          <span class="cooktime">
           25 mins
          </span>
         </p>
         <p class="single_recipe_text" style="color: #141517; font-size: 12px; padding: 0; margin: 4px;">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           Keywords:
          </span>
          bake cook appetizer entree dairy-free gluten-free turkey champagne
         </p>
         <p>
          <script type="text/javascript">
           // &lt;![CDATA[
document.write('&lt;ifr'+'ame s'+'rc="ht'+'tp://www.recipage.com/new_pageCreator/media_bar.php?recipe_id=6058229" width="100%" height="50px" fr'+'ameborder="0" scrolling="no"&gt;&lt;/ifr'+'ame&gt;');
// ]]&gt;
          </script>
         </p>
         <div id="ingredients">
          <p class="single_recipe_header" id="ingr_header" style="font-size: 18px; color: #b31212; text-decoration: none; padding: 0;">
           Ingredients
           <span class="single_recipe_text" style="font-size: 14px; color: #141517;">
            (Yields: about 1 dozen meatball)
           </span>
          </p>
          <ul class="single_recipe_text" id="ingr" style="color: #141517; font-size: 14px;">
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            <strong>
             For the meatballs:
            </strong>
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            1 lb ground turkey
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
             medium onion, finely chopped
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            1 rice cake, crumbled
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            1 egg
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            1/2 tsp salt
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            ground pepper
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            <strong>
             For the sauce:
            </strong>
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            1 can tomato paste
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
             can cranberries, whole
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
             tsp Dijon mustard
           </li>
           <li class="ingredient" style="margin-bottom: 3px;">
            1 cup champagne
           </li>
          </ul>
         </div>
         <div id="instructions">
          <p class="single_recipe_header" id="inst_header" style="font-size: 18px; color: #b31212; text-decoration: none; padding: 0;">
           Instructions
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           <strong>
            For the meatballs:
           </strong>
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           1. Preheat oven to 400 degrees F.
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           2. Combine all meatball ingredients and mix with hands.
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           3. Roll into 1 inch balls (or larger if serving as an entree) and place on a parchment or silicone-lined baking sheet.
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           4. Bake for 15 mins.
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           <strong>
            For the Sauce:
           </strong>
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           1. Combine all sauce ingredients in a large pot and cook on high until mixture begins to boil.
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           2. Add in meatballs and stir to coat.
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           3. Reduce heat to low and simmer, uncovered for 10 mins.
          </p>
          <p class="instruction">
           4. Place a toothpick in each meatball and serve as an appetizer.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="single_recipe_text" style="width: 100%; text-align: center; font-size: 10px; color: #141517;">
          Powered by
          <a class="single_recipe_header" href="http://www.recipage.com/" style="text-decoration: none; color: #b31212;" target="_blank">
           Recipage
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="single_recipe_text" style="width: 100%; text-align: center; font-size: 10px; color: #141517;">
          <a href="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs-31.jpg">
           <span class="pibfi_pinterest ">
            <img alt="champagne turkey meatballs 3" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-1416" height="453" src="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs-31.jpg" width="680"/>
            <span class="xc_pin" onclick="pin_this(event, 'http://pinterest.com/pin/create/button/?url=http://www.thehealthymaven.com/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs.html&amp;media=http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/12/champagne-turkey-meatballs-31.jpg&amp;description=Champagne Turkey Meatballs')">
            </span>
           </span>
          </a>
         </div>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Do you enjoy photography? What are your New Years plans?
          </strong>
         </p>
        </div>

             </p>
            </header>
            <div class="comment-content" itemprop="commentText">
             <p>
              Give it time
              <img alt=";)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://www.thehealthymaven.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/icon_wink.gif"/>
              Happy New Year to you too!
             </p>
